With `grpc.NewClient`, the connection doesn't have a timeout during creation - it's created immediately and made available. If we need the old behavior (block until connection is ready), we should use `grpc.WithBlock()` option.\n\n\nLooking at the actual usage patterns in the codebase, most places either already use `grpc.WithBlock()` or don't require synchronous connection establishment. For cases with timeout contexts created specifically for the Dial operation, the behavior will differ since `grpc.NewClient()` establishes connections asynchronously. {\\n390: \\treturn e.cfg\\n391: }\\n392: \\n393: // Close gracefully shuts down all servers/listeners.\\n394: // Client requests will be terminated with request timeout.\\n395: // After timeout, enforce remaning requests be closed immediately.\\n396: //\\n397: // The rough workflow to shut down etcd:\\n398: //  1. close the `stopc` channel, so that all error handlers (child\\n399: //     goroutines) won't send back any errors anymore;\\n400: //  2. stop the http and grpc servers gracefully, within request timeout;\\n401: //  3. close all client and metrics listeners, so that etcd server\\n402: //     stops receiving any new connection;\\n403: //  4. call the cancel function to close the gateway context, so that\\n404: //     all gateway connections are closed.\\n405: //  5. stop etcd server gracefully, and ensure the main raft loop\\n406: //     goroutine is stopped;\\n407: //  6. stop all peer listeners, so that it stops receiving peer connections\\n408: //     and messages (wait up to 1-second);\\n409: //  7. wait for all child goroutines (i.e. client handlers, peer handlers\\n410: //     and metrics handlers) to exit;\\n411: //  8. close the `errc` channel to release the resource. Note that it's only\\n412: //     safe to close the `errc` after step 7 above is done, otherwise the\\n413: //     child goroutines may send errors back to already closed `errc` channel.\\n414: func (e *Etcd) Close() {\\n415: \\tfields := []zap.Field{\\n416: \\t\\tzap.String(\\\"name\\\", e.cfg.Name),\\n417: \\t\\tzap.String(\\\"data-dir\\\", e.cfg.Dir),\\n418: e.GetLogger()\\n422: \\tlg.Info(\\\"closing etcd server\\\", fields...)\\n423: \\tdefer func() {\\n424: \\t\\tlg.Info(\\\"closed etcd server\\\", fields...)\\n425: \\t\\tverify.MustVerifyIfEnabled(verify.Config{\\n426: \\t\\t\\tLogger:     lg,\\n427: \\t\\t\\tDataDir:    e.cfg.Dir,\\n428: \\t\\t\\tExactIndex: false,\\n429: \\t\\t})\\n430: \\t\\tlg.Sync()\\n431: \\t}()\\n432: \\n433: \\te.closeOnce.Do(func() {\\n434: \\t\\tclose(e.stopc)\\n435: \\t})\\n436: \\n437: \\t// close client requests with request timeout\\n438: \\ttimeout := 2 * time.Second\\n439: \\tif e.Server != nil {\\n440: \\t\\ttimeout = e.Server.Cfg.ReqTimeout()\\n441: \\t}\\n442: \\tfor _, sctx := range e.sctxs {\\n443: \\t\\tfor ss := range sctx.serversC {\\n444: \\t\\t\\tctx, cancel \\t\\tsctx.cancel()\\n452: \\t}\\n453: \\n454: \\tfor i := range e.Clients {\\n455: \\t\\tif e.Clients[i] != nil {\\n456: \\t\\t\\te.Clients[i].Close()\\n457: \\t\\t}\\n458: \\t}\\n459: \\n460: \\tfor \\t\\te.tracingExporterShutdown()\\n467: \\t}\\n468: \\n469: \\t// close rafthttp transports\\n470: \\tif e.Server != nil {\\n471: \\t\\te.Server.Stop()\\n472: \\t}\\n473: \\n474: \\t// close all idle \\t\\te.wg.Wait()\\n484: \\t\\tclose(e.errc)\\n485: \\t}\\n486: }\\n487: \\n488: func stopServers(ctx context.Context, ss *servers) {\\n489: \\t// first, close the http.Server\\n490: \\tif ss.http != This context was used for:\n   - Timeout during connection establishment\n   - Cancellation of connection attempts\n\n   With `grpc.NewClient()`, these operations are no longer parameterized by context. The `grpc.WithBlock()` option can still be used to wait for connection readiness.\n\n2. **Backward Compatibility**: All existing dial options (e.g., `grpc.WithTransportCredentials()`, `grpc.WithBlock()`, etc.) continue to work with `grpc.NewClient()`.\n\n3. **Error Handling**: The error handling patterns remain unchanged - both functions return `(*grpc.ClientConn, error)`.\n\n4. **Deprecated Comment Removal**: Where present, the `//nolint:staticcheck` comments indicating deprecation are preserved for now, as they may be removed in future versions.\n\n5. **Excluded Files**:\n   - Vendor files (auto-generated protobuf files) were excluded\n   - Proto definitions were not modified per the requirements\n\n## Verification\n\nTo apply the patch:\n```bash\ncd /path/to/repo && git apply /logs/agent/patch.diff\n```\n\nTo verify the changes:\n```bash\ngrep -r \"grpc\\.Dial(\" . --include=\"*.go\" | grep -v vendor | grep -v \"grpc.NewClient\"\ngrep -r \"grpc\\.DialContext(\" . --include=\"*.go\" | grep -v vendor | grep -v \"grpc.NewClient\"\n```\n\nBoth commands should return no results if all migrations are complete.\n\n## Summary\n\nThis migration standardizes gRPC connection creation across three major Go projects (etcd, Kubernetes, and containerd) by adopting the newer `grpc.NewClient()` API.
